# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-29 22:00:25.551186

### Base Program

```py
def gcd(a, b):
    if b == 0:
        return a
    return gcd(b, a % b)

def count_GCD_subarrays(nums, k):
    count = 0

    for i in range(len(nums)):
        gcd_so_far = 0
        for j in range(i, len(nums)):
            gcd_so_far = gcd(gcd_so_far, nums[j])
            if gcd_so_far == k:
                count += 1

    return count
```

### Input

```json
[64, 53]
```

<details>
<summary>Parser Result: Passed ✅</summary>

Message: 
```
Success
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def gcd(a, b):
    if b == 0:
        return a
    return gcd(b, a % b)

def count_GCD_subarrays(nums, k):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(nums)):
        gcd_so_far = 0
        for j in range(i, len(nums)):
            gcd_so_far = gcd(gcd_so_far, nums[j])
            if gcd_so_far == k:
                count += 1
    return count
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def gcd(var_0, var_1):
    if var_1 == 0:
        return var_0
    return gcd(var_1, var_0 % var_1)

def count_GCD_subarrays(var_2, var_3):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(var_2)):
        gcd_so_far = 0
        for j in range(i, len(var_2)):
            gcd_so_far = gcd(gcd_so_far, var_2[j])
            if gcd_so_far == var_3:
                count += 1
    return count
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def gcd(var_4, var_5):
    if var_5 == 0:
        return var_4
    return gcd(var_5, var_4 % var_5)

def count_GCD_subarrays(var_6, var_7):
    count = 0
    for i in range(len(var_6)):
        gcd_so_far = 0
        for j in range(i, len(var_6)):
            gcd_so_far = gcd(gcd_so_far, var_6[j])
            if gcd_so_far == var_7:
                count += 1
    return count
```
